Such populations include: HIV-positive persons, recent contacts of TB case patients, patients with fibrotic changes on chest radiographs consistent with prior TB, patients with organ transplants and other immunosuppressed patients receiving the equivalent of >15 mg/day of prednisone for one month or more. ~ ~Reactions of 10 mm - Should be considered positive for individuals with an  increased probability of recent infection or who have conditions (other than HIV or pharmacologic immunosuppression) that increase the risk for TB including:~Recent (within the last five years) immigrants from high prevalence countries, such as areas of Eastern Europe, Latin America, Asia, and Africa, injection drug users who are HIV-negative or with an unknown HIV status. However, if these persons are tested because of entry into a work site where a high risk for exposure to TB is anticipated and a longitudinal tuberculin testing program is in place, a criterion of 15 mm of induration is recommended as a positive response.~ ~BOOSTER PHENOMENON - in some individuals, an initially falsely negative tuberculin test can be boosted to a true positive test by the skin testing procedure itself. This generally occurs among people in whom tuberculosis infection has occurred many years before and whose delayed type hypersensitivity reaction has diminished with time and in patients with a history of BCG vaccination. Administration of a TST to this population can restore reactivity, boosting the response to future TSTs."

Topics covered: ~- Wash feet every day with lukewarm water and mild soap~- Keep skin on feet smooth by applying cream or lanolin lotion~- Check both feet every day. The use of a mirror may be needed to see the bottoms of the feet.~- Do not treat calluses , corns or bunions without talking to your PCM first~- Cut toenails straight across to avoid ingrown toenails. File the edges of your toenails carefully.~- Do not  let your feet get too hot or too cold~- Do not go barefoot even indoors~- Shoes: do not wear shoes without socks, open toed shoes or shoes with pointed toes, avoid high heels~- Wear padded socks/stockings. Do not wear stretch socks, nylon socks, socks with an elastic bands/garter at the top.
